    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">I'll
start with most welcome news - <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">the rig
mobilization</font> (from the Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 wellsite to the Ma&#8217;anit-Joseph
#3 wellsite) <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">has
begun</font>, as you can see in the pictures below.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
current schedule indicates an <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">August 17 - 19, 2010</font> spud date
window for the new well and the latest news regarding rig mobilization sustains
that date.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Since my
last update to you (on July 23, 2010) we have almost completed the site
construction for the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In the
past week, I visited the new wellsite, so here are some photographs (from August
3rd, 4th and 5th) showing that the site has been almost fully prepared. As I
walked around the site, I saw that everything was very much in good order. Due
to all the prior planning, our staff and contractors are now implementing their
site construction work in a very calm and professional manner.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><img src="pic-9.jpg" alt=""></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The

(Aug 5, 2010)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">So, our
operations department is moving into high gear, as we all look forward to being
back in daily drilling operations very soon.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Here is
the latest, more detailed, news on Operations:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Joseph
#3 Well (M-J #3)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Well site
construction has continued to be the primary activity ongoing at the
Ma'anit-Joseph #3 well for the past two weeks.&#160;&#160;The work done by our
general contractor for this site was successfully concluded last week and the
remaining work is now being handled by our local roustabout crew, under the
watchful eye of Zion&#8217;s field manager. This remaining work includes the placement
of mobile units that will serve as field offices and laboratories; installation
of lighting and power generation facilities; installation of safety and security
equipment; and various other location enhancements that will make the wellsite
ready for continuous drilling operations.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In
addition to finalizing our drill site, work has begun on the installation of an
&#8220;acoustic wall&#8221;.&#160;&#160;This structure will mitigate sound effects from our
drilling operations, so that the surrounding communities are not adversely
affected by our drilling operations.&#160;&#160;Completion of the acoustic wall
installation is expected to occur concurrent with our spud date for the new
well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Mobilization
of the drilling rig from its temporary storage at the Ma&#8217;anit-Rehoboth #2
wellsite began this week.&#160;&#160;Full mobilization and rig-up will require
approximately 10 &#8211; 12 days. It is good to see our rig crew staff back after the
short absence following completion of their work on the Ma&#8217;anit-Rehoboth #2
well.&#160;&#160;With the crew back on site and the rig beginning its move, we
anticipate that drilling operations will soon commence.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Equipment
and well services continue to be procured and received.&#160;&#160;We have
experienced a few short delays in the anticipated receipt of some equipment
which could impact the timing of when we spud the well.&#160;&#160;Still, we
remain optimistic that our spud date will occur at mid-month and are now
projecting a specific time frame for this spud date of August 17 &#8211;
19.</font></div><br>

      <div id="FTR">

      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The
Issachar-Zebulun Permit Area</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
previously reported, on June 16, 2010, field acquisition of new 2-dimensional
seismic in the Jordan River Valley section of our Issachar-Zebulun permit area
was successfully concluded.&#160;&#160;Approximately 30 km of new seismic data
was collected on Zion's behalf by the Geophysical Institute of Israel
(GII).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This data
continues to be processed by a geophysical consultant in the United States, and
now also GII, into usable graphic imagery that can then be interpreted by our
geologists in their investigation for future drilling prospects.&#160;&#160;The
processing and interpretation of this data is expected to be finalized by
October 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Elijah #3
Well</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
previously noted, the Elijah #3 well was drilled to a depth of approximately
10,938 feet (3,334 meters) when the drill string became stuck within the Asher
Volcanics section of the hole. After recovering a significant portion of the
stuck drill pipe, progress in recovering the remainder of the pipe slowed and
the decision was made to temporarily suspend drilling operations pending further
analysis of the situation. <font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #000000">As</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #000000"> there were questions regarding the
volcanic rock that caused the stuck pipe, we decided to acquire additional field
seismic data in order to help to resolve questions regarding the
geology.</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On June
30, 2010, GII successfully concluded field acquisition of approximately 25 km of
new 2-dimensional seismic data within the Elijah #3 project
area.&#160;&#160;This data will help us to resolve certain questions regarding
the geology of the area surrounding this well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;As
with the seismic data collected in the Issachar-Zebulun permit area, this data
will also need to be processed and subsequently interpreted.&#160;&#160;In this
case, however, we are not looking for new prospects but instead looking for
greater clarity in the geology that underlies our Elijah-3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Processing
of the Elijah #3 seismic data is now underway and is being done by both GII and
a geophysical consultant in the United States.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 Well
(M-R #2)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This well
is currently temporarily suspended for possible future use as an offset well to
the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 (M-J #3) well which is to be drilled a short distance
away.</font></div><br>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>

      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">It is
important to note that we are drilling to the deep "Permian" structure in the
M-J #3 well; whereas the various intervals tested in the M-R #2 well consisted
of shallower and younger age rocks. As such, and despite the relative proximity
of these two wells, the results of the M-R #2 well tests are not necessarily
correlative to what we expect in the Permian of the M-J #3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">"In

for your support of Zion, and</font></div>
